<script type="text/javascript">
function setCookie(name, value, days){
    var date = new Date();
	var expires = '';
	if (days != 0) {
		date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
		expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
	}
    document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + ";path=/";
}
function getParam(p){
	var match = RegExp('[?&]' + p + '=([^&]*)').exec(window.location.search);
	return match && decodeURIComponent(match[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
}
var gclid = getParam('gclid');
if(gclid){
    var gclsrc = getParam('gclsrc');
    if(!gclsrc || gclsrc.indexOf('aw') !== -1){
		setCookie('gclid', gclid, 90);
	}
}
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
function readCookie(name) {
	var n = name + "=";
	var cookie = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < cookie.length;i++) {
		var c = cookie[i];
		while (c.charAt(0)==' '){c = c.substring(1,c.length);}
		if (c.indexOf(n) == 0){return c.substring(n.length,c.length);}
	}
	return null;
}

// Timofey сохранение в заказе UTM меток 22.12.2017
var sourceFrom = getParam('from');
var sourceUtm = getParam('utm_source');
var campaignUtm = getParam('utm_campaign');
var termUtm = getParam('utm_term');
var mediumUtm = getParam('utm_medium');
var contentUtm = getParam('utm_content');
if(!sourceUtm && document.referrer) {
	var referrer = document.referrer.replace(/^(?:https?:\/\/)?(?:[^@\n]+@)?(?:www\.)?([^:\/\n]+).*$/im, '</body>');
	if (referrer != '' && referrer != 'vstroyka-solo.ru' && referrer != 'adm.vstroyka-solo.ru') {
		sourceUtm = referrer;
		campaignUtm = 'referrer';
		termUtm = '';
		mediumUtm = 'link';
		contentUtm = '';
	}
}
if(sourceFrom && !readCookie("from")) {
	setCookie('from', sourceFrom, 180);
}
if(sourceUtm && !readCookie("utm_source")) {
	setCookie('utm_source', sourceUtm, 180);
	if(campaignUtm && !readCookie("utm_campaign")) {
		setCookie('utm_campaign', campaignUtm, 180);
	}
	if(termUtm && !readCookie("utm_term")) {
		setCookie('utm_term', termUtm, 180);
	}
	if(mediumUtm && !readCookie("utm_medium")) {
		setCookie('utm_medium', mediumUtm, 180);
	}
	if(contentUtm && !readCookie("utm_content")) {
		setCookie('utm_content', contentUtm, 180);
	}
}
// Timofey конец сохранение в заказе UTM меток 22.12.2017
// Timofey сохранение в заказе последних UTM меток 21.12.2018
if(sourceUtm && !readCookie("last_utm_source")) {
	setCookie('last_utm_source', sourceUtm, 0);
	if(campaignUtm && !readCookie("last_utm_campaign")) {
		setCookie('last_utm_campaign', campaignUtm, 0);
	}
	if(termUtm && !readCookie("last_utm_term")) {
		setCookie('last_utm_term', termUtm, 0);
	}
	if(mediumUtm && !readCookie("last_utm_medium")) {
		setCookie('last_utm_medium', mediumUtm, 0);
	}
	if(contentUtm && !readCookie("last_utm_content")) {
		setCookie('last_utm_content', contentUtm, 0);
	}
}
var leadGoodId = '0';
var leadCategoryId = '0';
var leadBrandId = '0';
var leadPageId = '0';
var leadRequestUri = window.location.href;
var leadReferrer = document.referrer;
if(!readCookie("leadFirstGoodId")) {
	// Берём из UTM меток, чтобы восстановить данные по старым клиентам
	var leadFirstGoodIdFromUtm = 1*readCookie("utm_term");
	setCookie('leadFirstGoodId', (leadFirstGoodIdFromUtm > 0 ? leadFirstGoodIdFromUtm : leadGoodId), 180);
}
if(!readCookie("leadLastGoodId")) {
	setCookie('leadLastGoodId', leadGoodId, 0);
}
if(!readCookie("leadFirstCategoryId")) {
	setCookie('leadFirstCategoryId', leadCategoryId, 180);
}
if(!readCookie("leadLastCategoryId")) {
	setCookie('leadLastCategoryId', leadCategoryId, 0);
}
if(!readCookie("leadFirstBrandId")) {
	setCookie('leadFirstBrandId', leadBrandId, 180);
}
if(!readCookie("leadLastBrandId")) {
	setCookie('leadLastBrandId', leadBrandId, 0);
}
if(!readCookie("leadFirstPageId")) {
	setCookie('leadFirstPageId', leadPageId, 180);
}
if(!readCookie("leadLastPageId")) {
	setCookie('leadLastPageId', leadPageId, 0);
}
if(!readCookie("leadLastReferrer")) {
	setCookie('leadLastReferrer', leadReferrer.substring(0, 1000), 0);
}
if(!readCookie("leadLastRequestUri")) {
	setCookie('leadLastRequestUri', leadRequestUri.substring(0, 1000), 0);
}

// Timofey конец сохранение в заказе последних UTM меток 21.12.2018

					event.preventDefault();
					element = $(this);

						type: 'GET',
						url: element.attr('href'),

						}
					});
					return false;
				});

	  $(document).on('order.cart.add', function(event, goodId, goodName, goodPrice, goodBrand, goodCategory, goodQuantity){
			/* Возможно лучше тут ga('ec:addProduct', {
			  'id': goodId,
			  'name': goodName,
			  'category': goodCategory,
			  'brand': goodBrand,
			  'price': goodPrice,

			});
			*/

				// Бывает, что не успевает загрузиться счётчик.
				$(document).on('ga.load', function() {
					ga('send', 'event', 'buttons', 'clickAddToCart');
				});
			}
		  console.log('g.cart.add');
	  });
	  $(document).on('order.after.create', function(event, orderId, orderTotal, orderProducts, email){
		  $(document).on('ga.load', function(){

				window.google_conversion_id = 881262350;
				window.google_conversion_language = 'en';
				window.google_conversion_format = '3';
				window.google_conversion_color = 'ffffff';
				window.google_conversion_label = 'bOogCIOmhWkQjv6bpAM';
				window.google_conversion_value = orderTotal;
				window.google_conversion_currency = 'RUB';
				window.google_remarketing_only = false;

				var a = document.createElement('script');
				var m = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
				a.async = 1;
				a.src = window.location.protocol + '//www.googleadservices.com/pagead/conversion_async.js';
				m.parentNode.insertBefore(a, m);

				for (productIndex in orderProducts) {
					var product = orderProducts[productIndex];
					ga('ec:addProduct', {
					  'id': product.id,
					  'name': product.name,
					  'category': product.category,
					  'brand': product.brand,
					  'price': product.price,
					  'quantity': product.quantity
					});
				}

				ga('ec:setAction', 'purchase', {
				  'id': orderId,
				});

			  ga('send', 'event', 'forms', 'formOrder');
			  console.log('g.order.save');
		  });
	  });
